Union"], "published-print": {"date-parts": [[1990]]}, "abstract": "<jats:p>The FU Orionis phenomenon has attracted increasing attention in recent years, and is now accepted as a crucial element in the early evolution of low mass stars. The general characteristics of FUors are outlined and individual members of the class are discussed. The discovery of a new FUor, BBW 76, is presented, together with a discussion of photometric and spectroscopic observations of the star. The evidence for circumstellar disks around T Tauri stars is briefly outlined, and the FUor phenomenon is discussed in the context of a disk accretion model. A large increase in the accretion rate through a circumstellar disk makes the disk self-luminous with a luminosity two or more orders larger than that of the star. Massive cool winds rise from FUors, and it is conceivable that they are related to the initiation of Herbig-Haro flows. The FUor phenomenon appears to be repetitive, and newborn low-mass stars may be cycling between the FUor state and the T Tauri state.</jats:p>", "DOI": "10.1017/s0074180900187789", "type": "journal-article", "created": {"date-parts": [[2019, 6, 7]], "date-time": "2019-06-07T22:38:48Z", "timestamp": 1559947128000}, "page": "229-251", "source": "Crossref", "is-referenced-by-count": 0, "title": ["Fu Orionis eruptions and early stellar evolution"], "prefix": "10.1017", "volume": "137", "author": [{"given": "Bo", "family": "Reipurth", "sequence": "first", "affiliation": []}], "member": "56", "published-online": {"date-parts": [[2016, 9, 23]]}, "reference": [{"key": "S0074180900187789_ref47", "DOI": "10.1086/146540", "doi-asserted-by": "publisher"}, {"key": "S0074180900187789_ref94", "unstructured": "Reipurth B. , Olberg M. , Booth R. : 1990, in preparation"}, {"key": "S0074180900187789_ref48", "DOI": "10.1086/190050", "doi-asserted-by": "publisher"}, {"key": "S0074180900187789_ref25", "DOI": "10.1086/158691", "doi-asserted-by": "publisher"}, {"key": "S0074180900187789_ref10", "DOI": "10.1086/185008", "doi-asserted-by": "publisher"}, {"key": "S0074180900187789_ref5", "author": "Bastian", "volume": "144", "first-page": "57", "year": "1985", "journal-title": "Astron.
